<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><i><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">This current report includes

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="font-weight:bold;margin:12.0pt 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Section 2 &#151;
Financial Information</font></b></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;margin:12.0pt 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 2.01&#160; Completion of Acquisition or
Disposition of Assets</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">On December 16, 2004, Mission Energy
Holding Company&#146;s subsidiary, Edison Mission Energy (EME), completed the sale
of the stock and related assets of MEC&nbsp;International&nbsp;B.V. (MECIBV)
pursuant to a Purchase Agreement, dated July&nbsp;29, 2004, by and between EME
and a consortium comprised of International Power plc (70%) and Mitsui &amp;
Co., Ltd. (30%), referred to as IPM. The Purchase Agreement was entered into
following a competitive bidding process. The sale of MECIBV included the sale
of EME&#146;s interests in ten electric power generating projects or companies
located in Europe, Asia, Australia, and Puerto Rico.&#160; As discussed further below, EME&#146;s interests
in the CBK, Tri Energy and Doga projects were excluded from the sale.&#160; Consideration from the sale of MECIBV and
related assets was $2.0&nbsp;billion in cash. The cash proceeds from the sale,
net of transaction costs and taxes, may be used by EME to repay debt, to
support contracting and hedges of power sales, to make capital expenditures for
its remaining domestic projects and for investment.&#160; In anticipation of the sale, the remaining
$200&nbsp;million of the $800&nbsp;million secured loan at Mission Energy
Holdings International, Inc., another subsidiary of EME, was repaid on December
14, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">On December&nbsp;16, 2004, EME issued
a press release announcing that it had completed the sale. A copy of the press
release has been attached under Item 9.01(c) as Exhibit&nbsp;99.1. Such
information is incorporated herein by reference.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;font-family:Times New Roman;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">EME has entered into a Purchase Agreement, dated as of
November 5, 2004 (the &#147;CBK PSA&#148;) with its partner in the CBK project, IMPSA S.A
to sell EME&#146;s interest in the CBK project to them.&#160; EME and IMPSA executed the CBK PSA following
IMPSA&#146;s exercise of its right of first refusal under the </font><font size="2" color="black" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">terms</font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;"> of the shareholders agreement for the
CBK project.&#160; Accordingly, the price,
terms and conditions set forth in the CBK PSA are substantially the same as
those set forth in the MECIBV transaction.&#160;
EME has also entered into a separate Purchase Agreement with IPM to sell
EME&#146;s interest in the CBK project to them if the sale to IMPSA is not
completed. Further, EME has entered into separate Purchase Agreements with IPM
concerning the Tri Energy and Doga projects. Anticipated proceeds from these
three projects will be approximately $216&nbsp;million. EME expects the sale of
its interests in the CBK, Tri Energy and Doga projects will be completed before
year end or in early 2005.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="font-weight:bold;margin:12.0pt 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Section 9 &#151;
Financial Statements and Exhibits</font></b></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;margin:12.0pt 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Item 9.01&#160; Financial Statements and Exhibits</font></b></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">(a)&#160; Financial Statements of Businesses Acquired</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">Not
applicable.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">(b)&#160; Pro Forma Financial Information</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">The
unaudited pro forma condensed consolidated financial statements of Mission
Energy Holding Company are attached as Exhibit 99.2.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">(c)&#160; Exhibits</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .75in;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">99.1&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; Press
Release of Edison Mission Energy, dated December 16, 2004.</font></p>

<p style="color:black;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-autospace:none;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

Company.</font></p>

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Exhibit&nbsp;99.1</font></b></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div align="center">

<table border="0" cellspacing="0" cellpadding="0" width="100%" style="border-collapse:collapse;width:100.0%;">
 <tr>
  <td width="50%" valign="top" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:50.0%;">

  </td>
  <td width="50%" valign="bottom" style="padding:0in .7pt 0in .7pt;width:50.0%;">
  <p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><i><font size="6" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:22.0pt;font-style:italic;">News Release</font></i></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

</div>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><b><i><u><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;font-style:italic;font-weight:bold;">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</font></u></i></b></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Contact:&#160; Kevin Kelley, </font></b><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">(626) 302-1033</font></p>

<p align="right" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:right;"><i><u><font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:9.0pt;font-style:italic;">www.edisonnews.com</font></u></i></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="5" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:16.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Edison
Mission Energy and Edison International</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="5" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:16.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Announce
Completion of the</font></b></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><b><font size="5" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:16.0pt;font-weight:bold;">Sale
of EME&#146;s Dutch Holding Company</font></b></p>

<h4 align="left" style="color:red;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;font-weight:normal;">&nbsp;</font></b></h4>

<p align="left" style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">IRVINE,
Calif. (USA), December 16, 2004 &#151; Edison Mission Energy (EME)</font> and its parent Edison International (NYSE:
EIX) today announced that EME has completed the sale of its
international power generation portfolio, owned by a Dutch holding company
which EME refers to as the &#147;BV,&#148; to a consortium comprised of International
Power plc (70%) and Mitsui &amp; Co., Ltd (30%).&#160; The closing of the sale of the BV includes 10
of the 13 international projects included in the Purchase and Sale Agreement
announced July 30th, one of the remaining three being purchased by a project
partner pursuant to a right of first refusal (CBK in the Philippines) and the
other two being projects (Tri-Energy in Thailand and Doga in Turkey) for which
project level consents could not be obtained in time for the sale of the BV.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:12.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Consideration
from the sale of the BV was approximately $2.0 billion in cash, representing a
base purchase price of $2.3 billion after adjustments for project distributions
received by EME during 2004, other working capital adjustments and the omission
of the three projects from the 13 contemplated in the original sale agreement.&#160; T</font>ogether with the closing of the sale of its interest in Contact Energy,
completed September 30, the sale by EME of its international assets is now substantially complete and has resulted thus far in the
receipt of total cash proceeds in the amount of $2.7
billion.&#160; The total cash proceeds, net of
transaction costs and taxes related to sale, will be available to repay debt, to
support contracting and hedges of power sales, to make capital expenditures for
EME&#146;s remaining domestic projects and for investment.&#160; In anticipation of the sale of the BV, the
remaining $200 million of the original $800&nbsp;million secured loan at
Mission Energy Holdings International, Inc. was repaid.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">The BV sale is the result of
a previously announced process to sell EME&#146;s portfolio of 14 international
energy assets located in Europe, the Asia Pacific region and Puerto Rico. &#160;&#160;Sale of&#160;
EME&#146;s remaining three international assets are expected to be finalized
before year end or early in the new year.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.5in;"><font size="3" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:12.0pt;">Lehman Brothers and Credit
Suisse First Boston acted as financial advisors to EME on the sale of its
international assets.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0in;"><font size="3" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:12.0pt;">###</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-indent:.5in;"><i><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;font-style:italic;">Edison
Mission Energy is a subsidiary of Rosemead, Calif.-based Edison International.&#160; Other Edison International companies include
Edison Capital and Southern California Edison.</font></i></p>

<p align="center" style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<div align="left" style="color:black;line-height:normal;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" color="black" face="Times New Roman" style="color:windowtext;font-size:10.0pt;">

<hr size="2" width="100%" noshade color="gray" align="left">

<html>

<head>





</head>

<body lang="EN-US">

<div style="font-family:Times New Roman;">

<p align="right" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Exhibit 99.2</font></b></p>

<p align="right" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:right;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:center;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">UNAUDITED PRO FORMA CONDENSED CONSOLIDATED FINANCIAL
STATEMENTS</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="font-weight:bold;margin:0in 0in .0001pt;page-break-after:avoid;text-align:left;"><b><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></b></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The following unaudited
pro forma condensed consolidated financial statements of Mission Energy Holding
Company (MEHC) are included herein:</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:justify;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1.<font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font></font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pro forma Condensed Consolidated Balance Sheet as of
September&nbsp;30, 2004</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2.<font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font></font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pro forma Condensed Consolidated Statement of Operations
for the nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2004</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">3.<font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font></font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pro forma Condensed Consolidated Statement of Income
(Loss) for the year ended December 31, 2003</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">4.<font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font></font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pro forma Condensed Consolidated Statement of Income (Loss)
for the year ended December 31, 2002</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">5.<font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font></font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pro forma Condensed Consolidated Statement of Income
for the year ended December 31, 2001</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">6.<font size="1" face="Times New Roman" style="font:7.0pt 'Times New Roman';">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</font></font><font size="2" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Notes to the Pro Forma Condensed Consolidated
Financial Statements</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The above-referenced unaudited
pro forma condensed consolidated financial statements reflect the sale of MEC
International B.V. and related assets.&#160; As
previously described in Item 2.01 of this report, on December 16, 2004, Edison
Mission Energy (EME) completed the sale of its international power generation
portfolio (excluding its interests in the CBK, Tri Energy and Doga projects) to
a consortium comprised of International Power plc and Mitsui &amp; Co.,
Ltd.&#160; Net proceeds from the sale of MEC
International B.V. may be used by EME to repay debt, to support contracting and
hedges of power sales, to make capital expenditures for its remaining domestic
projects and for investment.&#160; In
anticipation of the sale, Mission Energy Holdings International, Inc. repaid on
December 14, 2004 the remaining $200 million of the $800 million secured loan
that was funded on December 11, 2003.</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The unaudited pro forma
condensed consolidated financial statements have been prepared by applying
pro&nbsp;forma adjustments to the consolidated financial statements included in
MEHC&#146;s Annual Report on Form 10-K for the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2003 and
Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q for the nine-month period ended
September&nbsp;30, 2004. The unaudited pro forma condensed consolidated balance
sheet reflects the sale of MEC International B.V., assuming the transaction had
been consummated as of September&nbsp;30, 2004. Under the Purchase Agreement
for the sale of MEC International B.V., EME was required to liquidate a
partnership that held an ownership interest in two international projects.&#160; The liquidation of this partnership, together
with dividends that were paid prior to December 16, 2004, has been combined
with the sale of the stock of MEC International B.V. in preparing the pro forma
balance sheet at September 30, 2004.&#160; On
October 22, 2004, The America Jobs Creation Act of 2004 (Act) was enacted
which, among other things, includes a provision regarding repatriation of
foreign dividends.&#160; Since this Act was
not effective at September 30, 2004, the potential benefits related to
repatriation of foreign dividends prior to completion of sale of MEC
International B.V. are not reflected in the pro forma balance sheet set forth
herein. The estimated gain on sale for purposes of these unaudited pro forma
condensed consolidated financial statements will ultimately differ from the
actual gain to be recorded in the quarter ending December&nbsp;31, 2004. The
unaudited pro forma condensed consolidated statements of income reflect the
sale of MEC International B.V., assuming the transaction had been consummated
as of the beginning of the fiscal period presented. MEHC accounted for the
disposition as discontinued operations in its Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q for
the quarter ended September&nbsp;30, 2004 in accordance with Statement of Financial
Accounting Standards No.&nbsp;144, &#147;Accounting for the Impairment or Disposal
of Long-Lived Assets&#148; (SFAS 144). &#160;MEC
International B.V. was included in Income from Continuing Operations for the years
ended December&nbsp;31, 2003, 2002 and 2001 because SFAS&nbsp;144 criteria requiring
discontinued operations presentation had not been met during these periods.</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">1</font></p>

</div>

<br clear="all" style="page-break-before:always;">


<div>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">On September 30, 2004,
EME completed the sale of Universal Holdings to Origin Energy New Zealand
Limited.&#160; The sale of Universal Holdings
included the sale of EME&#146;s 51.2% ownership interest in Contact Energy Ltd.&#160; MEHC filed a Current Report on Form 8-K dated
October 4, 2004 with unaudited pro forma condensed financial statements that
reflected the sale of Universal Holdings. Universal Holdings&#146; operating results
were included in Income from Continuing Operations for the years ended
December&nbsp;31, 2003, 2002 and 2001 because SFAS&nbsp;144 criteria requiring
discontinued operations presentation had not been met during these periods.&#160; Accordingly, the unaudited pro forma
consolidated statements of income included herein also include the sale of
Universal Holdings in order to present pro forma consolidated operating results
that assume the completion of both transactions described above had been
completed as of the beginning of the fiscal period presented. </font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">Pro forma adjustments
have also been included to eliminate the operating results of the CBK, Tri Energy
and Doga projects, which were reclassified as discontinued operations in MEHC&#146;s
Quarterly Report on Form 10-Q for the quarter ended September&nbsp;30, 2004 in
accordance with SFAS 144. &#160;However,
operating results were included in Income from Continuing Operations for the
years ended December&nbsp;31, 2003, 2002 and 2001 because SFAS&nbsp;144 criteria
requiring discontinued operations presentation had not been met during these
periods.&#160; Accordingly, pro forma
adjustments are included to eliminate these results from continuing operations
for the years ended December&nbsp;31, 2003, 2002 and 2001. </font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:left;text-indent:.25in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">The pro forma adjustments
as described in the notes to the unaudited pro forma condensed consolidated
financial statements are estimates based on currently available information and
certain adjustments that management believes are reasonable. The unaudited pro forma
condensed consolidated financial statements are presented for informational
purposes only and are not necessarily indicative of the financial position or
operating results that would have occurred had the sale of MEC International
B.V. and Universal Holdings been consummated on, or as of, the dates indicated,
nor are they necessarily indicative of MEHC&#146;s future operating results or
financial position. The unaudited pro forma condensed consolidated financial
statements should be read in conjunction with the historical financial
statements of MEHC included in its Annual Report on Form&nbsp;10-K for
the year ended December&nbsp;31, 2003 and MEHC&#146;s Quarterly Report on
Form&nbsp;10-Q for the quarter ended September&nbsp;30, 2004.</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">2</font></p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:11.0pt;margin:6.0pt 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">(B)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Primarily reflects the

issue costs and elimination of accrued interest related to the early repayment
of the secured loan.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:11.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">(C)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Reflects
the elimination of the results of Universal Holdings for the period.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:11.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">(D)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Reflects
the elimination of the results of MEC International B.V. for the period.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:11.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">(E)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Reflects
pro forma decrease in interest expense resulting from the repayment of debt
utilizing cash proceeds primarily from the sale of Universal Holdings.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">&#160;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:11.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">(F)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Reflects
the income tax effects of the pro forma adjustments at the statutory or actual
tax rate.</p>

<p align="left" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman">&nbsp;</font></p>

<p align="left" style="font-size:11.0pt;margin:0in 0in .0001pt .5in;text-align:left;text-indent:-.5in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:11.0pt;">(G)</font><font size="1" style="font-size:3.0pt;">&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160; </font>Reflects
exclusion of results of CBK, Tri Energy and Doga projects from continuing
operations.&#160; These projects have been
classified as discontinued operations in the 2004 Third Quarter Report on Form
10-Q. </p>

<p align="center" style="margin:0in 0in .0001pt;text-align:center;text-indent:0in;"><font size="2" face="Times New Roman" style="font-size:10.0pt;">&nbsp;</font></p>
